// 数据过滤优化 const filteredData = trendData.filter(item => { return (!selectedShop || item.shop === selectedShop) && (!selectedCategory || item.category === selectedCategory) && (!selectedProduct || item.product === selectedProduct); }); // 数据聚合优化 const aggregatedData = {}; filteredData.forEach(item => { const date = item.date; if (!aggregatedData[date]) { aggregatedData[date] = 0; } aggregatedData[date] += item.amount || 0; }); const dates = Object.keys(aggregatedData).sort(); const amounts = dates.map(date => aggregatedData[date]); chart.data.labels = dates; chart.data.datasets = [{ label: '销售额', data: amounts, backgroundColor: 'rgba(54, 162, 235, 0.6)', borderColor: 'rgba(54, 162, 235, 1)', borderWidth: 1 }]; chart.update('none'); // 禁用动画提升性能 }, 100); // 更新过滤器选项 function updateFilters() { // 收集所有唯一值 trendData.forEach(item => { allShops.add(item.shop); allCategories.add(item.category); allProducts.add(item.product); }); tableBody.innerHTML = html; } // 获取品类下的单品数据 function getCategoryProducts(category) { // 统计该品类下的单品数据 const productStats = {}; trendData.forEach(item => { if (item.category === category) { const product = item.product || ''; // 过滤掉含有运费、室外机、赠品、虚拟字样的单品 if (product.includes('运费') || product.includes('室外机') || product.includes('赠品') || product.includes('虚拟')) { return; } if (!productStats[product]) { productStats[product] = { amount: 0, qty: 0 }; } productStats[product].amount += item.amount || 0; productStats[product].qty += item.qty || 0; } }); // 按销售额排序 const sortedProducts = Object.entries(productStats) .sort((a, b) => b[1].amount - a[1].amount) .slice(0, 20); let html = ''; sortedProducts.forEach(([product, data], index) => { const price = data.qty > 0 ? Math.round(data.amount / data.qty) : 0; html += `
📦 ${index + 1}. ${product} ─ 销售额: ¥${data.amount.toLocaleString()} | 销量: ${data.qty.toLocaleString()}件 | 单价: ¥${price.toLocaleString()}
`; }); return html || '

Set(); let allCategories = new Set(); let allProducts = new Set(); function initChart() { const ctx = document.getElementById('trendChart').getContext('2d'); chart = new Chart(ctx, { type: 'bar', data: { labels: [], datasets: [] }, options: { responsive: true, interaction: { mode: 'point', intersect: true }, onClick: function(event, elements) { if (elements.length > 0) { const element = elements[0]; const datasetIndex = element.datasetIndex; const index = element.index; const date = chart.data.labels[index]; showDateDetails(date); } }, plugins: { title: { display: true, text: '销售趋势' }, legend: { display: false }, tooltip: { mode: 'point', intersect: true, callbacks: { label: function(context) { if (context.dataset.type === 'line') { return context.dataset.label + ': ' + context.parsed.y + '件'; } else { return context.dataset.label + ': ¥' + context.parsed.y.toLocaleString(); } } } } }, scales: { x: { stacked: true }, y: { type: 'linear', display: true, position: 'left', stacked: true, beginAtZero: true, title: { display: true, text: '销售额 (¥)' } }, y1: { type: 'linear', display: true, position: 'right', beginAtZero: true, title: { display: true, text: '销量 (件)' }, grid: { drawOnChartArea: false } } } } }); // 初始化筛选选项 initFilters(); } function initFilters() { if (!trendData || trendData.length === 0) return; // 收集所有唯一值 trendData.forEach(item => { if (item.shop) allShops.add(item.shop); if (item.category) allCategories.add(item.category); if (item.product) allProducts.add(item.product); }); // 填充品类选项（按销售额排序） populateCategoryOptions(); // 填充店铺选项（按销售额排序） populateShopOptions(); // 填充单品选项（按销量排序） populateProductOptions(); } function populateCategoryOptions(selectedShop = 'all') { const categorySelect = document.getElementById('selCategory'); const currentValue = categorySelect.value; // 计算品类销售额 const categoryStats = {}; trendData.forEach(item => { if (selectedShop === 'all' || item.shop === selectedShop) { if (!categoryStats[item.category]) { categoryStats[item.category] = 0; } categoryStats[item.category] += item.amount || 0; } }); // 按销售额排序 const sortedCategories = Object.keys(categoryStats).sort((a, b) => categoryStats[b] - categoryStats[a]); // 重新填充选项 categorySelect.innerHTML = ''; sortedCategories.forEach(category => { const option = document.createElement('option'); option.value = category; option.textContent = category; categorySelect.appendChild(option); }); // 恢复之前的选择 if (currentValue && sortedCategories.includes(currentValue)) { categorySelect.value = currentValue; } } function populateShopOptions(selectedCategory = 'all') { const shopSelect = document.getElementById('selShop'); const currentValue = shopSelect.value; // 计算店铺销售额 const shopStats = {}; trendData.forEach(item => { if (selectedCategory === 'all' || item.category === selectedCategory) { if (!shopStats[item.shop]) { shopStats[item.shop] = 0; } shopStats[item.shop] += item.amount || 0; } }); // 按销售额排序 const sortedShops = Object.keys(shopStats).sort((a, b) => shopStats[b] - shopStats[a]); // 重新填充选项 shopSelect.innerHTML = ''; sortedShops.forEach(shop => { const option = document.createElement('option'); option.value = shop; option.textContent = shop; shopSelect.appendChild(option); }); // 恢复之前的选择 if (currentValue && sortedShops.includes(currentValue)) { shopSelect.value = currentValue; } } function populateProductOptions(selectedCategory = 'all', selectedShop = 'all') { const productSelect = document.getElementById('selProduct'); const currentValue = productSelect.value; // 计算单品销量 const productStats = {}; trendData.forEach(item => { if ((selectedCategory === 'all' || item.category === selectedCategory) && (selectedShop === 'all' || item.shop === selectedShop)) { // 过滤掉含有运费、室外机、赠品、虚拟字样的单品 const product = item.product || ''; if (product.includes('运费') || product.includes('室外机') || product.includes('赠品') || product.includes('虚拟')) { return; // 跳过这些单品 } if (!productStats[item.product]) { productStats[item.product] = 0; } productStats[item.product] += item.qty || 0; } }); // 按销量排序 const sortedProducts = Object.keys(productStats).sort((a, b) => productStats[b] - productStats[a]); // 重新填充选项 productSelect.innerHTML = ''; sortedProducts.forEach(product => { const option = document.createElement('option'); option.value = product; option.textContent = product; productSelect.appendChild(option); }); // 恢复之前的选择 if (currentValue && sortedProducts.includes(currentValue)) { productSelect.value = currentValue; } } function updateFilters(changedFilter) { const selectedCategory = document.getElementById('selCategory').value; const selectedShop = document.getElementById('selShop').value; if (changedFilter === 'category') { // 品类变化时，重新排序店铺和单品 populateShopOptions(selectedCategory); populateProductOptions(selectedCategory, selectedShop); } else if (changedFilter === 'shop') { // 店铺变化时，重新排序品类和单品 populateCategoryOptions(selectedShop); populateProductOptions(selectedCategory, selectedShop); } } function updateChart() { if (!trendData || trendData.length === 0) return; const selectedShop = document.getElementById('selShop').value; const selectedCategory = document.getElementById('selCategory').value; const selectedProduct = document.getElementById('selProduct').value; // 确定堆积维度 let stackDimension; if (selectedCategory === 'all' && selectedShop === 'all' && selectedProduct === 'all') { stackDimension = 'category'; // 默认按品类堆积 } else if (selectedCategory !== 'all' && selectedShop === 'all') { stackDimension = 'shop'; // 选中品类时按店铺堆积 } else if (selectedShop !== 'all' && selectedCategory === 'all') { stackDimension = 'product'; // 选中店铺时按单品堆积 } else if (selectedCategory === 'all' && selectedShop === 'all' && selectedProduct !== 'all') { stackDimension = 'shop'; // 只选单品时按店铺堆积 } else { stackDimension = 'product'; // 其他情况按单品堆积 } // 过滤数据 let filteredData = trendData.filter(item => { return (selectedShop === 'all' || item.shop === selectedShop) && (selectedCategory === 'all' || item.category === selectedCategory) && (selectedProduct === 'all' || item.product === selectedProduct); }); // 按日期和堆积维度聚合数据 const aggregatedData = {}; const stackItems = new Set(); filteredData.forEach(item => { const date = item.date; const stackKey = item[stackDimension]; if (!aggregatedData[date]) { aggregatedData[date] = {}; } if (!aggregatedData[date][stackKey]) { aggregatedData[date][stackKey] = { amount: 0, qty: 0 }; } aggregatedData[date][stackKey].amount += item.amount || 0; aggregatedData[date][stackKey].qty += item.qty || 0; stackItems.add(stackKey); }); // 排序日期和堆积项 const sortedDates = Object.keys(aggregatedData).sort(); const sortedStackItems = Array.from(stackItems).sort(); // 生成颜色 const colors = [ '#FF6384', '#36A2EB', '#FFCE56', '#4BC0C0', '#9966FF', '#FF9F40', '#FF6384', '#C9CBCF', '#4BC0C0', '#FF6384', '#36A2EB', '#FFCE56', '#4BC0C0', '#9966FF', '#FF9F40' ]; // 构建数据集 const datasets = []; // 计算各分段近30天累计金额用于排序 const stackItemTotals = {}; sortedStackItems.forEach(stackItem => { let total = 0; sortedDates.forEach(date => { total += aggregatedData[date][stackItem] ? aggregatedData[date][stackItem].amount : 0; }); stackItemTotals[stackItem] = total; }); // 按近30天累计金额从大到小排序（图表中从下往上显示） const sortedByAmount = sortedStackItems.sort((a, b) => stackItemTotals[b] - stackItemTotals[a]); // 堆积柱状图数据集（销售额） sortedByAmount.forEach((stackItem, index) => { const data = sortedDates.map(date => { return aggregatedData[date][stackItem] ? aggregatedData[date][stackItem].amount : 0; }); datasets.push({ label: stackItem, data: data, backgroundColor: colors[index % colors.length], borderColor: colors[index % colors.length], borderWidth: 1, type: 'bar', stack: 'amount' }); }); // 折线图数据集（销量） const qtyData = sortedDates.map(date => { let totalQty = 0; Object.values(aggregatedData[date] || {}).forEach(item => { totalQty += item.qty; }); return totalQty; }); datasets.push({ label: '销量', data: qtyData, borderColor: '#FF6384', backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 99, 132, 0.1)', borderWidth: 2, type: 'line', yAxisID: 'y1', tension: 0.1, fill: false }); // 更新图表 - 去掉年份显示 chart.data.labels = sortedDates.map(date => { const d = new Date(date); return (d.getMonth() + 1) + '-' + d.getDate().toString().padStart(2, '0'); }); chart.data.datasets = datasets; chart.update(); // 更新默认数据表格 updateDefaultDataTable(); } function showDateDetails(date) { if (!trendData || trendData.length === 0) return; const selectedShop = document.getElementById('selShop').value; const selectedCategory = document.getElementById('selCategory').value; const selectedProduct = document.getElementById('selProduct').value; // 过滤当天数据 let dayData = trendData.filter(item => { return item.date === date && (selectedShop === 'all' || item.shop === selectedShop) && (selectedCategory === 'all' || item.category === selectedCategory) && (selectedProduct === 'all' || item.product === selectedProduct); }); // 确定显示维度 let displayDimension; if (selectedCategory === 'all' && selectedShop === 'all' && selectedProduct === 'all') { displayDimension = 'category'; } else if (selectedCategory !== 'all' && selectedShop === 'all') { displayDimension = 'shop'; } else if (selectedShop !== 'all' && selectedCategory === 'all') { displayDimension = 'product'; } else if (selectedCategory === 'all' && selectedShop === 'all' && selectedProduct !== 'all') { displayDimension = 'shop'; } else { displayDimension = 'product'; } // 聚合数据 const aggregated = {}; dayData.forEach(item => { const key = item[displayDimension]; // 如果显示维度是单品，过滤掉含有运费、室外机、赠品、虚拟字样的单品 if (displayDimension === 'product') { const product = item.product || ''; if (product.includes('运费') || product.includes('室外机') || product.includes('赠品') || product.includes('虚拟')) { return; // 跳过这些单品 } } if (!aggregated[key]) { aggregated[key] = { amount: 0, qty: 0 }; } aggregated[key].amount += item.amount || 0; aggregated[key].qty += item.qty || 0; }); // 生成表格 - 格式化日期去掉年份 const d = new Date(date); const formattedDate = (d.getMonth() + 1) + '-' + d.getDate().toString().padStart(2, '0'); let tableHtml = `

${formattedDate} 详细数据

`; // 按销售额排序 const sortedItems = Object.entries(aggregated) .sort((a, b) => b[1].amount - a[1].amount); sortedItems.forEach(([key, data]) => { tableHtml += ` `; }); tableHtml += `
${displayDimension === 'category' ? '品类' : displayDimension === 'shop' ? '店铺' : '单品'} 销售额 (¥) 销量 (件)
${key} ¥${data.amount.toLocaleString()} ${data.qty.toLocaleString()}
`; document.getElementById('detailsContainer').innerHTML = tableHtml; } function updateDefaultDataTable() { if (!trendData || trendData.length === 0) return; const selectedShop = document.getElementById('selShop').value; const selectedCategory = document.getElementById('selCategory').value; const selectedProduct = document.getElementById('selProduct').value; // 过滤数据 let filteredData = trendData.filter(item => { return (selectedShop === 'all' || item.shop === selectedShop) && (selectedCategory === 'all' || item.category === selectedCategory) && (selectedProduct === 'all' || item.product === selectedProduct); }); // 按日期聚合数据 const aggregatedData = {}; filteredData.forEach(item => { const date = item.date; if (!aggregatedData[date]) { aggregatedData[date] = { amount: 0, qty: 0 }; } aggregatedData[date].amount += item.amount || 0; aggregatedData[date].qty += item.qty || 0; }); // 排序日期 const sortedDates = Object.keys(aggregatedData).sort(); // 清空现有的日期列 const headerRow = document.getElementById('defaultTableHeader'); const salesAmountRow = document.getElementById('salesAmountRow'); const salesQtyRow = document.getElementById('salesQtyRow'); // 保留第一列，清空其他列 while (headerRow.children.length > 1) { headerRow.removeChild(headerRow.lastChild); } while (salesAmountRow.children.length > 1) { salesAmountRow.removeChild(salesAmountRow.lastChild); } while (salesQtyRow.children.length > 1) { salesQtyRow.removeChild(salesQtyRow.lastChild); } // 添加日期列和数据 sortedDates.forEach(date => { const data = aggregatedData[date]; // 格式化日期 - 去掉年份 const d = new Date(date); const formattedDate = (d.getMonth() + 1) + '-' + d.getDate().toString().padStart(2, '0'); // 添加日期表头 const headerCell = document.createElement('th'); headerCell.style.cssText = 'min-width: 80px; text-align: center; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #ddd; background-color: #f5f5f5;'; headerCell.textContent = formattedDate; headerRow.appendChild(headerCell); // 添加销售额数据（万元，0个小数点） const amountCell = document.createElement('td'); amountCell.style.cssText = 'text-align: center; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #ddd;'; const amountInWan = Math.round(data.amount / 10000); amountCell.textContent = amountInWan.toLocaleString(); salesAmountRow.appendChild(amountCell); // 添加销量数据 const qtyCell = document.createElement('td'); qtyCell.style.cssText = 'text-align: center; padding: 8px; border: 1px solid #ddd;'; qtyCell.textContent = data.qty.toLocaleString(); salesQtyRow.appendChild(qtyCell); }); } // 内联显示品类详情 function showCategoryDetailInline(buttonElement, category, type) { if (!category) return; // 更新按钮样式 - 找到当前按钮的父元素中的所有按钮 const buttonContainer = buttonElement.parentElement; const buttons = buttonContainer.querySelectorAll('button'); buttons.forEach(btn => { btn.style.background = '#6c757d'; // 默认灰色 }); buttonElement.style.background = '#007bff'; // 当前按钮蓝色 // 找到对应的内容容器 const contentContainer = document.querySelector(`.category-detail-content-${category.replace(/ /g, '_')}`); if (!contentContainer) return; // 生成对应的内容 if (type === 'shop') { contentContainer.innerHTML = generateCategoryShopRankingHtml(category); } else if (type === 'product') { contentContainer.innerHTML = generateCategoryProductRankingHtml(category); } } function generateCategoryShopRankingHtml(category) { if (!trendData || trendData.length === 0) return '

暂无数据

'; // 聚合该品类下的店铺数据 const shopStats = {}; trendData.forEach(item => { if (item.category === category) { if (!shopStats[item.shop]) { shopStats[item.shop] = { amount: 0, qty: 0 }; } shopStats[item.shop].amount += item.amount || 0; shopStats[item.shop].qty += item.qty || 0; } }); // 按销售额排序 const sortedShops = Object.entries(shopStats) .sort((a, b) => b[1].amount - a[1].amount) .slice(0, 20); let html = ''; sortedShops.forEach(([shop, data], index) => { const price = data.qty > 0 ? Math.round(data.amount / data.qty) : 0; html += `
🏪 ${index + 1}. ${shop} ─ 销售额: ¥${data.amount.toLocaleString()} | 销量: ${data.qty.toLocaleString()}件 | 单价: ¥${price.toLocaleString()}
`; }); return html || '

该品类下暂无店铺数据

'; } function generateCategoryProductRankingHtml(category) { if (!trendData || trendData.length === 0) return '

暂无数据

'; // 聚合该品类下的单品数据 const productStats = {}; trendData.forEach(item => { if (item.category === category) { const product = item.product || ''; // 过滤掉含有运费、室外机、赠品、虚拟字样的单品 if (product.includes('运费') || product.includes('室外机') || product.includes('赠品') || product.includes('虚拟')) { return; } if (!productStats[product]) { productStats[product] = { amount: 0, qty: 0 }; } productStats[product].amount += item.amount || 0; productStats[product].qty += item.qty || 0; } }); // 按销售额排序 const sortedProducts = Object.entries(productStats) .sort((a, b) => b[1].amount - a[1].amount) .slice(0, 20); let html = ''; sortedProducts.forEach(([product, data], index) => { const price = data.qty > 0 ? Math.round(data.amount / data.qty) : 0; html += `
📦 ${index + 1}. ${product} ─ 销售额: ¥${data.amount.toLocaleString()} | 销量: ${data.qty.toLocaleString()}件 | 单价: ¥${price.toLocaleString()}
`; }); return html || '

该品类下暂无单品数据

'; } // 初始化 document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { initChart(); updateChart(); // 初始化默认数据表格 updateDefaultDataTable(); });
